Mr. Moon's Selected Words
56
Mr. Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Path of the Pioneer
The church leaders and evangelism team leaders gathered here must now return and continue the activities they have been engaged in during the time the teacher was absent, whether through special prayers or other activities. Has a prayer period been set nationwide starting in May? "We are engaging in relay fasting and devotion." 
The Foundation for Church Development
As people who carry God with them, being devoted is akin to a lifeline. It is like connecting a water pipe to a water source, which means we must always put in effort. 
Moreover, from the perspective of the church leader responsible for the church, they must unite with three male and three female family members. If the seven people, including the church leader, do not become one in heart, the church will not develop. To unite with three people, one must not just align with those who share their thoughts. One should center around three people: someone who resonates well with them, someone they resonate the least with, and someone in between, always working together to ensure that the minister is supported. 
When a minister goes on a tour, they should not go alone. There must be someone praying for them from behind. There must be someone who prays for them. Furthermore, while the teacher is touring, if you are aware of where the teacher is going and pray and put in effort for that, then… God will surely be with those who engage in such activities. 
Likewise, a leader must have a base. They must engage in activities centered around that base, which must always be stronger than the local activities. Just as branches grow out from a tree trunk, the trunk must be larger than the branches. Similarly, the base where the church leader is situated must always be a powerful foundation compared to the local activities. Without such a foundation, development cannot occur. 
Therefore, the church leader must understand that the key to church development is how to ensure that three men and three women can work together as one for the church, and they must strengthen this system of activities. 
If one person forms a triad with three others, it automatically becomes 24 people. If a triad is formed around three people, it naturally becomes 12, and when the triads of three men and three women are combined, it naturally becomes 24. This means that a single subject must be tied together in an inseparable position. 
For this to happen, the church leader must consider how much effort they have put into those people, which will determine how much effort those people will put into the church leader. If the church leader does not invest any effort or establish connections, nothing will work no matter how hard they try. 
Therefore, the church leader must devote themselves to the church members and teach them. They must instruct them on what to do day and night, and put in effort. For a foundation of devotion to be established, there must always be a path. Opening that path cannot be done alone. Thus, the next step is to pave the way for the church members. If there are three people, it does not end there; they must form a triad. You must always think about how to expand the organization centered around the triad. 
If the church leader forms three women and three men around themselves, it becomes seven people. From this position, if they continue to form triads, they will naturally develop. Therefore, the organization of triads must be prioritized. 
The Role of the Church in the Community
Those who have formed triads must have the mindset that Unification Church members should always think about economic activities. If there are three people, they must consider how to engage in economic activities and manage their households. They must be educated on household management issues, that is, economic issues. 
Next, there is the issue of education; they must take turns being responsible for general education, our principles, ideological issues, etc. They must be capable of providing such training. In terms of education, child education and church education are important. Here, we can address overall issues such as life education and faith education. Such education must be provided, and the church women must fulfill a mission to become a foundation for supplying knowledge to society. 
Next is evangelism. Evangelism is a social activity, and one must be friendly with the people in the neighborhood wherever they go. Only by being friendly with the people in the neighborhood can new activities be initiated there. Thus, with issues of social activities, ideological preparedness, educational issues, and life issues, one must be equipped to evangelize. When it comes to evangelism, it is the responsibility of the minister… Based on that foundation, one must critique education for general families and also critique education for the church. The church's education must be of a higher standard than general social education. 
Therefore, ministers must supplement their sermons and always provide what is necessary and helpful to the church members. To elevate the level of the church members, the minister should not only have relationships with them but also invite local leaders or people who have studied in specialized fields to educate the church members. Of course, the spiritual aspect is important, but activities to elevate the general level must also be developed. For example, cultural projects… 
Just as general society people belong to various departments under the Republic of Korea, our church must also represent important departments of the central government of Korea and always consider what they can provide for the benefit of the entire life surrounding them. 
To do this, the church must discuss with the village head for the innovation of the neighborhood and also discuss with the township head for the innovation of the township, establishing private relationships. The church must become one that can focus on developing the village by building horizontal bridges with such people. The church must be like that. 
Our ideology is to establish a heavenly kingdom on earth, so it should not be a one-sided place that only focuses on faith. You must always think that without cultivating a high-level living training and a cultural life that serves as a model for society centered around the foundation of social life, you cannot succeed. 
Therefore, church leaders must read at least two or three magazines. They must read magazines about general society and read many books. You must always think about these issues and not only focus on church life but also consider the aspect of guiding general life. 
Moreover, since local people may not be well-informed about current affairs, they should read newspapers and provide current affairs explanations. This does not mean that they must do it directly. They should arrange for it to happen. Gather even the general neighborhood people and do it. That is evangelism. When people frequently visit the church, they become friendly. 
We will also engage in activities like farming in the future, but we will invite leaders to educate on all farming-related issues. We are planning such initiatives. Therefore, we must implement a touring system in various fields. However, we cannot do this without significant economic backing… Currently, we are talking about church mobilization teams and such, but in the future, we will create mobilization teams in various fields. We do not need a large number of people. If we can negotiate for two days with specialists in a region, we can create a mobilization team of about 40 to 50 people, equipped with mobility, and establish a nationwide organization centered around that field. 
In the future, without the church playing an intermediary role to elevate the level of each field, we cannot bring about overall social innovation. For that, a unified ideology is necessary. 
To carry out nationwide unified activities like this, the church must be the foundation. This means that individuals should not act independently. If the church is the foundation, it can unify activities and spread them nationwide, making it invaluable. Therefore, the ideological foundation is of utmost importance. This is absolute. 
Must Provide Benefits and Influence Society
From this perspective, the leaders of the Unification Church cannot be detached from society. If they can become the village head or township head with our support, that country will fall under our ideological realm. We must begin such movements from now on. 
Therefore, the church must not focus solely on principles. Of course, we must establish a strong foundation for faith life centered on principles, but alongside that, we must engage in social movements, especially education. The most important thing is education. We must do education well. From family education to public life in the village, we must be able to educate. Our church must influence in these areas so that everything revolves around the church. 
Church members cannot just be educated in faith and gather only on Sundays. 
Therefore, we must always study how to create an environment where village people can come to the church and discuss. To develop that village, the church leader must collaborate with the village head. Naturally, that will happen. The village head is responsible purely from a worldly perspective, while we are responsible from a heavenly perspective, so when the earthly leader and the heavenly leader fully engage with each other, that village cannot help but follow the determined path. It is possible to cooperate not only through the village head but also through the church. 
The village head can communicate with the township but cannot reach the county. Our church, however, has the capability for the church leader to communicate with the county and the province. Our church organization is a separate entity, capable of bringing people from the village to the headquarters to exert influence. In terms of organizational utilization, the church foundation can surpass general organizational systems. If that is the case, we can gather all the village heads across the nation at once and carry out various movements. 
Therefore, we must be able to unify internal and external relationships. Thus, we must not be in a position of dependency. We must always be at the forefront. We must influence either materially, mentally, or culturally. These are the issues at hand. 
To influence materially, there are improvements in farming. We must guide them on what can directly help their economic situation. Whether it is through farming methods or educational influences, we must provide benefits to them. If we cause them losses, they will not follow us. If we cause them losses, they will not follow. When the church has a path that can be beneficial in material, mental, or general educational aspects, and when positive content is disseminated, those involved will automatically be drawn in. That is how it works. 
Therefore, in the future, to become a minister, one must undergo comprehensive foundational education and be equipped in all aspects. Ultimately, what is a minister? A minister is a representative of God. Is God one-sided? God is the ultimate responsible leader who manages the entire world into a single ideal realm, so church leaders must also not only serve the church but be able to influence and discuss with people in all administrative fields, including local leaders. 
Until now, you have stood in a one-way, unilateral position. Because you have not established such relationships, you cannot solidify the overall organizational foundation of society. Generally, church members are specific individuals, such as women or those who are weak in society. When these people turn to religion and then lose those connections, they become completely isolated, unable to find their roots, and everything collapses. 
Therefore, you must always think about how our church institutions can not only guide the spiritual aspect but also present conditions that can positively influence the practical and educational aspects. When they feel that "the church is indispensable," naturally… the church is something they create. You must think about these multidimensional activities. 
If you cannot do these activities alone, if there are three churches under the county, the leaders of these three churches should come together and decide what each will specialize in, and then agree to support each other while touring. When three people collaborate, they can overcome challenges more effectively. Moreover, when three people cooperate, they can expand their reach significantly. 
Therefore, if there are five church leaders, each should research their respective fields and hold gatherings that can influence and provide benefits to their members. You must consider that without applying these issues, you will be isolated in social activities. You must be able to provide benefits and not be in a position of dependency. 
In terms of faith, you can provide benefits to them, which is why they follow you. If you become indebted to them, they will never follow you.
to me? You should know better than to act like this.’ (laughter) This is how you can gradually change their perspective.

In this way, you should not think of the established church pastors as unreachable. Approach them with a friendly demeanor, and when they oppose you, engage them in conversation. Ask them why they oppose, and remind them of the teachings that emphasize forgiveness and compassion. This can lead to a more open dialogue.

When you meet with them, start with humor and light-heartedness. This can help ease any tension and create a more comfortable atmosphere. As you continue these interactions, you may find that their initial resistance softens, allowing for more constructive conversations.

Ultimately, the goal is to build relationships and foster understanding. By doing so, you can create a foundation for collaboration and mutual support in the community. This is the essence of your mission: to engage with others, share your values, and work together for the common good.
Is that so? If someone is a bastard, they should be treated like a dog. That’s how you firmly tighten the grip and force them to surrender. They can’t move. It means you shouldn’t rush in and say not to do that. Looking at it this way, a man should have a bit of dignity. That’s true. The little ones just stay quiet. (laughter) 

Once, twice, or three times, it becomes a minus, so the youthful vigor doesn’t get worse. But if they keep chattering, saying, “What’s this? Pastor, is there anything special?” and keep babbling, it continues day after day. They just smile and stay quiet. So when it’s time to eat lunch, if you go to them, they’ll chase you away and you can’t eat. In the summer, when they eat lunch on the porch with the door open, you can sneak in and say, “I didn’t know the pastor’s life was this hard.” and “The life of a minister is truly pitiful. There aren’t many side dishes.” You take a serious stance and support them. When you’re eating, you can’t say anything about heresy. (laughter) If there aren’t enough side dishes, the next time you go, you bring some meat scraps with you. You have to strategize.

Everyone, try that kind of strategy. Then that person will definitely fall into that strategy after six months. To do that, you need to pave the way in the market streets, like in a thatched house or noodle shop. You do that, and when the pastor goes to the market, you follow him. You follow him, and when lunchtime comes, you know for sure he will go to this place, so you buy him a big bowl of noodles. 

The small market is obvious. At that time, you go to the noodle shop in advance and make a reservation. If I bring someone, I ask them to make it a double serving and pay in advance to treat them specially. Why? Because the money is the same, but I am close to this shop. Then it already fits in. “Hey, this young guy hasn’t been here long, but he’s already gotten friendly with the noodle shop, and even though he pays the same money, they treat him well.” This becomes a point of interest.

That’s why you need to strategize. You need to strategize. Is it a direct operation, a siege operation, or an indirect operation? A direct operation is when you show yourself, and an indirect operation is when you have a third party do it. If you do an indirect operation, you can make that person talk even in their bedroom. Their daughter and son can do that. You need to think about that. To do that, you need to study it.

You need to think about those aspects. To survive, one cannot ignore society and the environment they live in. Therefore, in that regard, you should always play a leading role. To do that, you need to cleverly do what is not done in that village. For example, you can start a grass-cutting movement or gather young people to promote compost production. Not only poor households but also wealthy ones need a lot of compost, so gather young people from the neighborhood and have them open their gates to bring in a load of compost to stack it up. If you do that once a month, you can mobilize the entire village.

You need to create a multi-dimensional activity system that can benefit all areas. If this happens, you can eat and live in that neighborhood without spending a penny. If there are elderly people, they will be curious and wait at the door, and the ladies will wait, and all the neighbors will wait. When you become this unspoken center, then the church will naturally thrive.

When it’s time for worship, you say, “The reason I come here and work hard is because I understood the holy will of heaven. People must honor heaven. This is the general climate of Korea, and even in honoring heaven, one must know and honor it. Isn’t it more wonderful to honor your parents knowingly rather than unknowingly? Because you must know and honor heaven, I will talk to you about those issues, so come and listen.” If you say that, it will happen naturally.

Everyone, you know about fishing, right? Have you ever caught fish in the countryside? Evangelism should be done like fishing. You can’t just sit quietly and think, “God, help me. Spirit world, cooperate.” and expect everything to work out while you close your eyes and wander around. At that time, the spirits in the spirit world will say, “You brat!” (laughter) Do you know what kind of spirits are in the spirit world (paradise)? They are people who sacrificed their lives while being beheaded…. “You brat, and you want help?” they would spit and turn away. It doesn’t work that way. So you need to strategize like you would when fishing.

When fishing, you can’t just stand alone; initially, men and women should hold hands tightly and whisper. But while doing this, you need to narrow down. (demonstrating) That’s how the fish get gathered; if you just whisper, they all escape. Because you’re alone, you have to spread your hands and play the whispering game. If you get tightly packed, not a single one can escape. It’s exactly like that. To do that, you need to make sure you can hold on until the end.

The longing for people is extremely precious. 

Everyone, try praying for one person. “If that person gets caught in my hands, I will make them a person within a few months.” Put your heart into nurturing that person. I have heard my mother say many times that the joy of raising a child is even greater than the joy of not having one. My mother gave birth to thirteen children. Having that many children is quite something, right? She raised eight of them, but she said that the time spent raising babies was the best. She suffered the most, couldn’t sleep at night, and sometimes dozed off during the day, but just seeing the baby brightened her world. Similarly, you should experience a joy greater than raising a child while nurturing your family.

In the early morning, you wait for someone to come…. You have to wait. In the morning, you wait for any family member to come, and sometimes you rush out…. There’s a saying, “If you open the door, they will be there,” but when you go out and find no one, you pray with a disappointed heart, and they will come. They will come. That’s how spiritual connections are made.

You might think, “I’m the church leader; they should come and find me.” But wait and see if they come. Even if you wait a thousand years, not a single person will come. If they’re not meant to come, will they come? The church leader who is easygoing and asks for things without hesitation, what will they come for? You need to put in effort. Longing for people….

When the teacher was in Beomil-dong, how much he longed for people that he would sit alone and mumble. There, a blank sheet of paper is covered. You can hear what the crowd is saying. You can hear it, but you can’t see their faces. If you just remove that one sheet of paper, the crowd can come. What you are longing for is heard…. That’s why you long for people. You wake up in the morning and lose track of time until evening, longing for people. Truly, the heart that longs for people is extremely precious. When that longing reaches its peak, people will come. When they come and you treat them with that heart, absolutely…. Since people are spiritual beings, if they try to stand up in that place, their legs will stiffen and they won’t be able to stand. It becomes a matter of life and death. It becomes strange. They become completely enveloped in that environment.

You need to understand that such a history existed at the beginning of the Unification Church. You must long for people. It’s not about your spouse and children. It’s about longing for people for the sake of the will. When someone passes by on the road at sunset, you wait with the hope that they will come to your house, and when that person takes the side road, you feel disappointed. With that kind of heart, you should contribute to that village. Then you will never be an absolute loner.

The teacher’s secret is nothing special. Even when he sees people with blonde hair and blue eyes in each country, he forgets the feeling of them being foreigners. Do you understand? Even though he speaks through an interpreter, he feels that they were all friends in the past. “We lived together back then, so aren’t we all the same? I should have been able to touch their hands and caress their bodies. Isn’t it a regret that I couldn’t?” Even at night, he wants to care for those people, just wanting to see them and wanting to be with them. This is the secret. Do you understand?

When I feel that heart, even if those people tell me not to be interested in them, I will be interested. Just as a person with a high antenna in the world of heart becomes the master, naturally, that environment will all be integrated. That’s how the world of heart works. When a person comes, instead of thinking, “Oh, here comes a thief,” you should think, “Even a thief is welcome.” If there’s a thief worse than a thief—who is an enemy thief—if that person is about to die at the hands of terrible villains, you will even feel pity for that enemy thief. That’s how it is. Isn’t it? Even if there’s an enemy thief, if he ends up in a situation where he’s about to be killed by terrible villains, you will feel sorry for that enemy. You won’t think, “Well, he deserves it!” When he’s below the limit of your anger, you might think, “He deserves it.” But if it goes beyond that, it flips.

So the question is how much I have dedicated my body and heart for others, how much I have longed for people. I still feel that way. When I see family members going to church barefoot, I cannot bear to look at their feet. I can’t look at them. This attitude of heart is extremely necessary. That is the heart of a parent. When they come with those bare feet, they must have come despite their pride, and when I see that, I feel a deep friendship in my heart, just like a mother’s heart.

Also, when the ladies come wearing skirts with big holes in them, I can’t see those holes. That heart, that person is not someone else. Isn’t that so? If it were your sister, your daughter, or your older sister, you wouldn’t be able to remain calm seeing that. Wherever you go, if you see them dressed improperly, you wouldn’t be able to lift your head. That heart is needed. Have you felt that way sometimes? When that happens, those people naturally blend in. If you think, “What’s this? They’re dressed like that,” you shouldn’t look at them as if they are someone else. You need to have the heart that they are not someone else.

The minister must first be like that. If you experience the spirit world, you will immediately understand. If you see a poor person and think, “You did well,” you will be punished. You shouldn’t think that way. The place where the heart is filled with the thought, “How can I help that person?” is the spirit world. It’s not a place where people boast about how great they are. Because it’s such a world, bowing your head comes naturally, and order is established automatically. That foundation of heart, that foundation of character is what you need.

Even when people who are struggling with their livelihood do evangelism, the teacher also did pioneering evangelism, but if you think, “I should evangelize wealthy people,” that’s wrong. You should think, “I should evangelize the people that heaven is looking for.” Do you understand? You might think you should evangelize wealthy people or capable people, but the people heaven is looking for are not wealthy or capable. Do you understand?

You should think, “I should evangelize the people heaven is looking for.” That person could be an illiterate grandmother. A grandmother who has no charm and no sociability…. Even if you give her potatoes, she will give them to you with a fist because that’s how they live, and they can be incredibly blunt. They are like unrefined gold ore that holds a lot of unrefined gold. To become rich, you need to find the vein. Just because a gold ring sparkles doesn’t mean it’s real; the gold embedded in the ore is real.

So when you meet such people, you shouldn’t think about your prestige or face. Even if you talk all night, it’s good. You will know once you start talking. When you talk to a person whom heaven loves, during the conversation, you will feel like you are reciting poetry. Do you understand what I mean? It feels like you are meeting people who are entering the ideal world in the realm of heart. The words spoken at that time are not worldly words. Whether they are elderly men or anyone else, even if you talk all night, it is sincere. When you experience that, the place where you sat becomes sacred. You need to experience that attitude of heart.

When you exchange such feelings, there will definitely be multiplication, and if you establish a subject-object relationship centered around such people, heaven will definitely cooperate. Don’t have the perspective that you had until now. You might think, “I used to give lectures in front of hundreds of people; can I talk to just one or two people?” but absolutely not! You need to understand that the real thing is only one. The real thing is one.

Putting in effort is not for the masses but for one person. God has not put in effort for the masses for 6,000 years; He has put in effort for one person. Isn’t that right? It was to find the lost Adam, one person. To find the completed Adam, He has been working hard until now, even forgetting thousands of years of history, to find that one real person. But if the masses shout “Wow!”? Even if there are ten million people who shout “Wow!” and then turn around and say “Deliver!” and all run away, they are useless. You need to understand that.

Everyone, a perfect seed is one by one. Each seed must be perfect. If I am a perfect seed, the question is how many perfect seeds I can create. Even if I die, I must always think about whether I can pass on this tradition and leave this will for my descendants. It’s not about many people. While your personal faith life and character are important, you must understand that you can only conclude that you lack multi-dimensional ability.

You need to look at your face and understand what type you are. What kind of person am I? You need to know yourself well. You need to know whether you are irritable or dull. I have what kind of talent! I have what kind of shortcomings! You need to know these things. The person in charge must be an enemy to those shortcomings. If those shortcomings have brought loss before heaven, you must repent until your bones melt. You must swear on your tongue that you will never act that way again. If there is such a place, it is wise to avoid that place immediately. Otherwise, you endure and overcome. You need to correct those things.

Good character must be cultivated. I have what strengths…. Then the question is how to connect those strengths to the masses. Connecting one person…
than they could eat. This is the tradition we have inherited from our ancestors. We should not resent those who eat at our door, nor should we turn them away. My father was like that. When beggars came, he would simply give them his meal. My grandfather was the same. He hosted many guests. If someone passing through the neighborhood asked to stay the night, he would say, “There’s a house belonging to someone named so-and-so, go and stay there.” He fed many people from all over the country. Moreover, people from Jeolla Province often received meals at our house.

This is the kind of heart we need to cultivate. If you do not have this foundation of heart, you cannot truly connect with others. You must have the desire to help others as if their troubles were your own. This is the essence of being a true leader and a true person of faith. You must be able to empathize with the suffering of others and act accordingly.

When you see someone suffering, you should feel compelled to help them. This is not just a matter of charity; it is a fundamental human responsibility. You must not only think of your own comfort but also of the well-being of others. This is the heart that God desires from us.

In your evangelism, do not choose who to approach based on their status or appearance. Everyone has a purpose for coming to you, and it is your responsibility to fulfill that purpose. If you fail to do so, you should feel remorse and strive to create another opportunity to help them.

Your eyes are dry. You have entered the path of faith, yet your tears have dried up. You should be able to shed tears of compassion for the suffering of others. When you see the plight of the thirty million people in this nation, how can you remain indifferent? Look at the mountains of Korea; they are bare and desolate. There is no other country in the world with such mountains. The Korean people are pitiful. When you consider our five-thousand-year history, it is a sad reality that we have never once shown our sovereignty to the world.

Now look around. To the west is China, to the north is Russia, to the east is Japan, and Korea is split in two. We are in a dire situation, caught between life and death. This is a serious time. Therefore, you must stand in this position and pray, “Heavenly Father, what will you do with this nation?”

The problems are immense. You must say, “With my meager strength, if I can contribute even a thread to your providential will, I will dedicate my utmost sincerity.” This is the attitude you should have. If you promise to wake up at a certain time and then oversleep by even a minute, you should shed tears of repentance. If you make a promise and fail to keep it by even a second, you should feel a sense of shame.

This mission is not developed through strategies or tactics but through the path of obedience. While strategies are necessary, they should not be aimed at harming others. Instead, they should be intended to benefit others and save their lives.

Do not be selective in your evangelism. Understand that everyone who comes to you has a purpose. You must fulfill that purpose completely. If you fail to do so, you should feel remorse and strive to create another opportunity to help them.

Your eyes are dry. You have entered the path of faith, and you should be able to shed tears of compassion. You must experience the depths of sorrow and anguish in your heart. Do you understand what I mean? You should cry so deeply that your lips swell and your mouth fills with tears.

Let us delve into the fundamental issue. Raise your hand if you have repented. Raise your hand if you feel you have completely settled your past sins. According to our restoration history, after the Old Testament and New Testament eras have been indemnified, there must be something left over to begin the era of the Completed Testament. This is the principle of Unification Church teachings. Even when considering the historical eras of the Old Testament and the time of Jesus, there must be something remaining after indemnification.

Therefore, I am carrying out the ideals that Jesus sought to fulfill. I am speaking of things that go beyond what Jesus spoke. Do you understand this, everyone?

Without resolving the mistakes of the Old Testament and New Testament eras, we cannot enter the Completed Testament era. Even now, when I speak with tears, you cannot compare to that. When I say “Father!” it is different from when you say it. The words may be the same, but the content is different. The question is whether you stand in a position that is completely settled before God.

This is why you must not treat people carelessly. Up until 1970, the headquarters of the association allowed anyone who was hungry to eat. It is not acceptable to look at someone eating and say, “Why are you eating?” Those who have come this far should not think that way. It is a human duty to feed the hungry. Even if the food is obtained through hard work, sharing it is a human obligation. If you have rice stored away and scold someone for eating it, that household will not last long.

We have been educated by our ancestors in this way. Do not resent those who eat at your door. My father was like that. When beggars came, he would simply give them his meal. My grandfather was the same. He hosted many guests. If someone passing through the neighborhood asked to stay the night, he would say, “There’s a house belonging to someone named so-and-so, go and stay there.” He fed many people from all over the country. Moreover, people from Jeolla Province often received meals at our house.
I ate and left. Whether they are from Gyeongsang-do or Jeolla-do, everyone did the same when fleeing to Manchuria. The place where we lived was about 3 ri away from the national road in Sinuiju, so it was a neighborhood in a very good location, and we hosted many people. Those traveling from Jeolla-do to Manchuria were selling rain gear, and we fed many of those merchants with public rice. But just feeding them public rice is not enough. At the same time as feeding public rice, one must also put forth a public spirit. That is the way to be blessed. Do you understand what I mean? 3) God and Our Humanity
If there are any first-time attendees here today, please raise your hands. And if there are those seeing the teacher for the first time, please raise your hands. Yes, please lower them. It’s hard to see because of the trees.

Clarifying the Existence of God is the Most Important Issue
Many humans live in this world. We understand that today’s world issues are not someone else’s problems but have entered an era of direct issues for us. Regardless of whether it is the democratic world or the communist world, everyone hopes for one world and a world of peace. However, we feel that it is impossible to achieve that one world and world of peace solely through humanity.

With human power, human wisdom, and human culture, we find ourselves at a point where we cannot hope for a true world of peace or a unified world.

From this perspective, what is the central issue in solving world problems? I believe that clarifying whether God exists or not is the most important issue. If all humanity knows that God exists, we will clearly understand what direction God’s will aims for, and when we know that will, that world will truly be one world, a world of peace, and an ideal world.

On the day we know that God exists, all problems in the communist world, democratic world, and everywhere will be resolved. When we know that God exists and understand His will, it is natural that humanity cannot help but follow that will.

Until now, there have been countless religions on this earth, but they have not been able to present the question of whether God truly exists or not. Considering that we can solve this fundamental problem, we will briefly discuss the topic "God and Our Humanity."

The question of whether God exists is a philosophical issue that humanity has sought to clarify and a problem that religions have pursued until now. Therefore, we must deal with God not from an abstract position but from a practical standpoint.

How Can We Know God Exists?
Now, let’s consider the question of how we know that God exists. God Himself is invisible. If there are those among you who have spiritual experiences, you will know that even when entering the spiritual world, God is not visible. We can predict that God exists through His actions, but we cannot see God with our own eyes.

Looking at this universe, scientists today say that this universe is a world of existence. They say, "The world exists." Then, what is necessary for existence? For existence, there must be a power behind it. This is something that anyone, regardless of who they are, can think of universally. Without power, there can be no existence. When we look at whether an existing object is causal or resultant, we see that the currently existing objects cannot be purely causal. There must be some absolute being or subject that has brought about the results through some cause. The existence that is brought about as a result must have power.

Now, when we consider whether power comes first or existence comes first, we see that there must be power before existence. Where there is no power, there can be no existence. Therefore, it becomes a problem that power must exist for existence to occur. Thus, we cannot deny that this vast universe is formed based on the expectation of power that can achieve this. Power must come first. We can think that it is not the visible material existence that comes first, but the invisible power that is the issue.

Furthermore, power itself cannot simply exist as it is. For power to continue to exist, it must act. Power can only exist in the place where it is acted upon. We know that we recognize electricity not by seeing electricity itself, but through the actions of electricity. Similarly, we come to understand that power cannot exist apart from the expectation of action.

Principles of Existence and Action
Now, in order for action to occur, what must happen? It cannot act alone. There is no such thing as acting alone in this universe. We reach the conclusion that a relative relationship is necessary for action to occur. Among that relationship, there must be a subject and an object. The action phenomenon occurs in the relationship of subject and object, and through that action phenomenon, power exists, and by virtue of that power, a being is formed.

Then, what is necessary as a prerequisite behind the power of existence? It is action. Action must take place. Furthermore, what is the prerequisite necessary for action to occur? There must be a subject and an object. We can deduce this through an inductive method. We cannot deny that action does not occur where the relationship of subject and object is not formed.

When the teacher standing here speaks to you, if he speaks without you being present, that is, without the relationship of subject and object, he would be considered insane. Moreover, in order for the subject and object to continue to have an ongoing reciprocal action, they must bring about results that are more beneficial to either the subject or the object. Only in that context can the action continue. If only one side of the subject and object shows a negative aspect, we can see that the action begins to decrease. 

The continuity of action is possible because the subject and object can hope for something that can be more positive. Only in that context can the action continue.
지, 마이너스될 수 있는 면을 바라보고 작용한다면 그것은 반드시 점점 작아지는 결과가 되기 때문에 없어지기 마련이라는 결론을 내릴 수 있습니다. 만일에 작은 것을 바라보고 작용하게 된다면 이 세계는 형성될 수 없다는 결론이 나오는 것입니다. 주체와 대상이 서로 보다 플러스될 수 있는 목적을 바라보며 작용하지 않고, 서로 작게 되는 목적을 바라보면서 작용한다는 원칙이 성립된다면 이 방대한 우주는 형성될 수 없다는 것입니다. 원소면 원소 하나를 중심삼고 볼 때, 그 원소가 어떠한 상대적 원소를 대하여 작용하는 데는, 그 원소보다도 작용하는 두 원소가 서로 나을 수 있는 하나의 목적을 지니고 작용하는 데서 계속적인 작용을 유지할 수 있는 것이지. 주체와 대상이 자기 자체보다 더 작아질 수 있는 무엇을 바라보고 작용한다는 원칙은 있을 수 없는 것입니다. 만일에 그렇게 된다면 이 우주는 형성되지 않는다는 것을 우리는 확실히 알아야 되겠습니다. 작용하는 데는 반드시 두 작용체, 주체와 대상이 보다 플러스될 수 있어야 합니다. 그런 데서만 작용을 한다는 사실을 우리는 여기에서 결론지을 수 있는 것입니다.

그렇기 때문에 작용하는 목적을 두고 보게 되면, 이는 플러스(주체)보다도 크고 마이너스(대상)보다도 큰 제3의 존재, 결과적 존재가 나오게 되는 것입니다. 오늘 여러분들이 여기에 집회가 있다고 해서 왔는데 이곳에 온 목적은 어디에 있느냐? 그것은 올 때의 그 마음보다도 더 플러스될 수 있는, 좀더 나을 수 있는 그 무엇을 찾아서 온 것입니다. 만일에 여기에 와 가지고 마이너스될 수 있는 결과를 가져온다면 그러한 작용은 점점점점 없어지게 마련인 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 이 현상세계에서 보여지는 모든 작용은 스스로를 감소시키기 위해서 작용하는 존재는 하나도 없다는 결론을 지을 수 있는 것입니다.

매일같이 시장에 나가는 주부가 있다고 하면, 그 주부가 시장에 나갈 때는 한푼이라도 손해 보기 위해서 나가는 사람은 없습니다. 나가는 데는 반드시 이익을 바라보고 나간다는 것입니다. 이 원칙이 자기 스스로 바라보는 목적으로 되어 있기 때문에 그런 계속적인 작용을 할 수 있는 것입니다. 만일 나가 가지고 자기가 바라는 목적이 연속적으로 이루어지는 사실을 바라볼 수 있게 될 때는 그 작용은 계속적으로 지속된다는 사실을 우리는 알 수 있습니다.

이런 관점에서 볼 때, 주체와 대상의 관계는 손해나는 자리에서는 작용하지 않는다는 것입니다. 이것이 우주의 천리요, 천칙(天則)이라는 것을 우리는 확실히 알아야 되겠습니다. 만약에 작아지는데도 작용한다면 거기에는 파탄이 벌어진다는 것을 여러분이 확실히 알아야 되겠습니다.

이런 관점에서, 친구지간에 합하는 것도 이것이 매양 아무 내용 없이 합하는 것이 아니라는 것입니다. 갑(甲)이라는 친구와 을(乙)이라는 친구가 합하는 것은 서로의 공동목적을 발견하는 데서 합하게 마련이고, 그 공동 목적이 서로에게 플러스될 수 있는, 이익 될 수 있는 입장으로 계속된다면 그 작용은 계속하는 것입니다. 만일에 여기에서 일면이라도 마이너스로만 나타나게 될 때는 그 작용은 점점점점 정지 상태로 내려간다는 것입니다. 이것은 우리의 일상생활에 있어서나, 혹은 사회의 모든 움직이는 조직체를 통해서, 혹은 국가간의 외교문제에서도 볼 수 있는 것입니다. 이러한 전체 문제는 스스로 이익 될 수 있는 일면을 발견하는 데서 작용하지, 그 이하의 자리에서는 작용하지 않는다는 원칙을 우리는 알아야만 되겠습니다.

남자 여자, 혹은 젊은 청년 남녀들이 서로서로 좋아하는 것을 보더라도, 서로가 대할 수 있는 과정을 거쳐 가지고 둘이 보다 이익 될 수 있는 서로의 그 무엇을 발견하는 자리에서는 서로서로 교제를 계속할 수 있는 것이지만, 만일에 교제를 계속하면 할수록 마이너스되는 입장에 서게 된다면 이 둘은 갈라지지 말라고 해도 자연히 갈라지게 마련이고, 둘의 사이는 보다 나쁜 결과에 도달하고 마는 것을 우리는 일상생활에서, 혹은 생활 주변에서 잘 느끼고 보는 것입니다.

그렇기 때문에 작용이라는 것은 주체와 대상 관계가 있어야 형성되는데, 그 작용이 계속되기 위해서는 주체와 대상이 서로 플러스될 수 있는 공동 목표하에서만이 계속되는 것이지, 그 이하에서는 작용이 이루어지지 않는다는 것입니다. 이것이 우주의 존재 철칙이요, 법칙이라는 것을 우리는 알아야만 되겠습니다.

또 화학을 공부하는 화학도가 실험실에서 자기가 목적하는 그 무엇을 연구하기 위해서, 갑이라는 원소와 을이라는 원소를 작용시키려고 아무리 힘을 가하고 아무리 노력해도 작용하지 않는 원소가 있는가 하면, 생각지도 않은 원소끼리는, 바라지도 않는데도 불구하고 서로서로가 작용을 하는 이런 결과를 많이 보게 되는 것입니다. 그건 왜 그러냐? 이 화학도는 자기가 바라는 그 목적을 이루기 위해서 원소와 원소를 합하려고 하지만, 그 원소 자체로 보게 될 때는 만일 작용을 하게 되면 그 원소 자체는 마이너스를 초래하는 결과가 된다는 것을 무엇보다도 그 원소 자체가 잘 알고 있다는 것입니다.

그러나 생각지도 않는 다른 원소끼리는 왜 합하게 되느냐? 그것은 플러스면 플러스 원소, 마이너스면 마이너스 원소가 서로 상대적 관계에 있어서 보다 나은 결과를 바라볼 수 있는 입장에 서게 되면 작용을 하지 말라고 해도 하기 마련이기 때문입니다. 그러므로 여기에서 우주의 존재 원칙을 규정지을 수 있는 것은 무엇이냐? 반드시 하나의 원소가 자기 자체보다도 나을 수 있는 결과를 추구하는 데서만이 작용이 성립된다는 원칙을 여러분이 알아야 되겠습니다. 그 이하가 될 수 있는 데서는 성립 안 된다는 것입니다. 만약에 마이너스되는 데서도 작용할 수 있는 천리원칙을 형성해 놓았다면 이 우주는 없어지고 마는 것입니다. 하나의 존재 원칙의 법칙적 기대가 오늘날 이러한 원칙에 따라 서게 되었다는 것을 우리는 생각해야 되겠습니다.

여러분, 그렇지 않아요? 친구를 중심삼고 그 친구 좋다 좋다 할 때, 두 사람의 사이가 손해나는 자리에서 좋다고 하는 사람은 없습니다. 어떤 면에서든지 플러스될 수 있는 면이 크면 클수록 오랜 세월 동안 친구의 입장을 계속 유지할 수 있는 것이지만, 대하면 대할수록 손해만 보게 되면 그 것은 갈라지지 말래도 갈라지고 맙니다. 끝장을 보지 말래도 끝장을 보게 마련인 것입니다. 이것이 존재의 원칙이라는 것을 여러분이 알아야 되겠습니다.

이러한 관점에서 볼 때, 모든 존재는 주체와 대상으로 되어 있습니다. 주체와 대상을 중심삼고 거기에는 끊임없이 작용을 함으로써 힘이 형성되고, 그 힘이 형성된 기대 위에서 모든 것이 존재한다는 것입니다. 그러면 하나의 원소는 어떻게 되는 것이냐? 물질의 최소 단위를 두고 보면 그 최소 단위가 원자인데, 그 원자는 어떻게 되어 있느냐? 전자와 양자를 중심삼아 가지고, 서로서로 상대적 관계를 중심삼고 운동을 하고 있는 것입니다. 그렇게 운동을 하는 것은 서로서로가 운동할 수 있는 어떠한 목적적인 그 무엇을 갖고 있기 때문입니다. 이와 같이 전자와 양자는 그 자체보다도 큰 것을 바라보고 서로가 운동을 한다는 것입니다. 여기에서 작용함으로써 보다 큰 것을 추구할 수 있는 최소 단위의 물질이 원자입니다. 그렇기 때문에 원소에는 여러 가지가 있는 것을 우리는 알고 있는 것입니다. 이런 관점에서 볼 때, 주체와 대상이 보다 나아질 수 있는 면을 바라보는 자리가 아니고서는 작용이 형성되지 않는다는 것을 여러분이 알아야만 되겠습니다.

하나님이 양심작용의 주체
우리 인간에게는 부정할래야 부정할 수 없는 양심이란 것이 있습니다. 양심이 있다는 것을 부정하는 사람은 없는 것입니다. 타락한 인간들은 하나님이 있는지 없는지 모르지만, 만일 하나님이 있다는 입장에서 보게 될 때, 그 하나님은 창조주요, 그 하나님이 지은 인간은 피조물인데, 그런 피조물과 창조주가 합할 수 없는, 하나의 공동목적을 제시할 수 있는 그 무엇이 있어야 됩니다. 하나님이 인간을 지었다면 그 지어진 인간이 하나님이 바라는 창조의 목적과 일치될 수 있는 그 점에 도달할 수 있는 어떤 힘의 작용체를 만들지 않고는 인간을 지을 수 없다는 결론을 내릴 수 있는 것입니다. 하나님은 절대자이시니 절대자인 하나님과 피조물인 우리 인간이 합할 수 있는 제1의 기반, 접촉할 수 있는 제1의 터전이 반드시 있어야 되는 것입니다.

그렇기 때문에 하나님은 인간을 대해서 그 목적하는 결과에 도달할 수 있게끔 우리 인간 가운데 작용할 수 있는 그 무엇을 존속시켜야 되는 것입니다. 그것이 없다면 하나님이 바라는 제3의 목적 기준 앞에 도달해서, 하나님도 기쁘고 인간도 좋아할 수 있는 자리를 발견할 수 없는 것은 당연한 이치인 것입니다. 절대적인 하나님이 우리 인간을 지을 때, 인간을 창조하던 창조목적의 기준과 지음 받은 우리 인간으로서 가야 할 목적의 기준은 서로 다를 수 없는 것입니다. 이것이 반드시 하나될 수 있는 데에서 하나님도 기뻐할 수 있는 것이요, 인간도 기뻐할 수 있다는 것을 생각하게 될 때, 인간 가운데 절대적인 하나님을 대신해서 그것을 찾아 올라갈 수 있는 무슨 작용이 있어야 된다는 것입니다. 그 작용이 없게 되면 도달할 수 없으니, 그것을 바라는 힘이 있어야 된다는 것입니다. 나를 끌고, 나를 자극시켜 가지고 끌어내어 밀어주는 힘이 있어야 됩니다. 그 힘이 무엇이냐 하면, 여러분이 부정할 수 없는 양심이라는 것입니다.

양심이 작용하는 데는 반드시 어떻게 작용하느냐 하면, 높아지기를 바라 고 작용하는 것입니다. 양심은 지금 현재의 자기보다 나아져라, 나아져라 하고 재촉하는 것입니다. 이 작용만은 부정할 수 없는 것입니다. 양심이 현재의 자기보다도 높아지라고 촉구하지, 현재의 자기보다도 낮아지라고 자기 자신 앞에 촉구하는 그런 작용은 하지 않는 것입니다. 오늘보다도 내일, 내일보다도 모레가 보다 나을 수 있게…. 금년보다도 내년, 혹은 10대보다도 20대, 20대보다도 30대, 가면 갈수록 더 높고 더 가치적인 자기를 형성하라고 추구시키는 그 힘이 양심작용인 것입니다. 이것은 여러분이 잘 아는 겁니다.

그러면 이게 왜 이렇게 작용하느냐? 아까 말하기를, 존재하기 위해서는 반드시 힘이 있어야 되고, 힘이 형성되기 위해서는 작용이 있어야 되고, 작용을 하기 위해서는 주체와 대상이 있어야 된다고 했습니다. 이것이 존재를 위한 하나의 원칙입니다. 이렇게 보게 될 때 우리 양심은 틀림없이 작용을 하고 있는 것입니다. 양심은 어릴 때부터 늙어 죽을 때까지 일생 동안 작용하는 것입니다. 그러면 양심은 혼자 작용하느냐, 그렇지 않으면 양심이 작용할 수 있는 다른 상대적 존재가 있느냐? 이것을 지금까지 인간들은 생각하지 않았습니다.

작용하는 데는 반드시 주체와 대상 관계가 형성되어 있어야 합니다. 그렇지 않고는 작용이 안 됩니다. 전기를 보면 플러스 마이너스가 있는데, 그것이 서로 연결되지 않으면 결코 작용하지 않습니다.

이와 마찬가지로 우리에게는 양심이 있다는 것은 그 누구도 부정할 수 없고, 양심이 작용을 계속하고 있다는 것도 부정할 수 없습니다. 그리고 양심이 작용을 계속하는 데는 반드시 주체와 대상의 관계가 있어야 하는데, 그 주체와 대상의 관계를 확실히 모르고 있습니다. 양심이 있는 것을 알고 있는데…. 작용하고 있는 그 무엇, 주체가 되는 그 무엇이 없어 가지고는 작용을 계속할 수 없는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 양심 자체를 두고 그 양심이 주체냐 대상이냐 하는 것을 생각해 볼 때, 우리 인간의 양심은 어디까지나 대상적인 존재지 주체적인 존재는 아니라는 것입니다.

그렇기 때문에 그 무엇인지는 모르지만 작용의 원칙을 따라 찾아보게 될 때, 반드시 작용하지 않을 수 없는 하나의 주체가 있어야 됩니다. 그 주체와 대상은 손해나는, 서로가 마이너스되는 것을 바라보고 작용하는 것이 아니라, 보다 플러스될 수 있는, 보다 나을 수 있는 것을 향해서 작용하는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 여러분의 양심작용은 보다 나을 수 있는 것, 보다 큰 것, 가치적인 것, 보다 세계적인 것을 향해서 작용하고 있다는 것입니다. 이렇게 보다 플러스될 수 있는 그 길을 찾아 나서는 양심이 있는 것을 부정할 수 없는 것입니다. 따라서 양심작용은 혼자 하는 것이 아니라, 주체와 대상 관계의 공동 목적점을 바라보고 작용한다고 결론지을 수 있는 것입니다.

사랑은 행복과 생명의 근원
하나님이 있다면, 하나님이 이 우주 전체의 주체라면 그 주체 앞에 상대적 관계에 있는 존재물이 어디에 가서 합해지느냐? 합해질 수 있는 일치점이 반드시 이 우주 가운데 있어야 되고, 하나님과 인간 가운데 있어야 되는 것입니다. 그 일치될 수 있는 종착점이 무엇이냐? 그게 문제라구요. 우리 인간이 제일 바라는 것은 무엇이냐? 인간은 행복하기를 바랍니다. 그러면 행복은 어떠한 것이 행복이냐? 혼자서 행복하다고 생각하는 사람은 없습니다. ‘아, 행복이야, 뭐 나 혼자 있으면 행복하지….’ 이러겠지만, 행복이라는 명사 자체가 자기 홀로 행복하다는 것은 절대 아닙니다. 어떠한 남자가 있으면 그 남자 앞에 반드시 상대적 존재가 있어야 행복이라는 말이 성립되는 것입니다. 여자면 여자 앞에, 남자면 남자 앞에 주체와 대상 관계가 하나되는 자리를 기반으로 하여 행복을 추구하려고 하지, 그 자리를 떠나 가지고 행복을 추구하는 사람은 없는 것입니다. 만약에 그 자리를 떠나 가지고 행복을 추구한다고 하는 남자가 있다면 그 남자는 100년 이내에, 1세기 이내에 망해 버리고 맙니다. 끝장을 보고 마는 것입니다.

행복을 꿈을 꾸되 반드시 주체와 대상 관계를 중심삼아야 합니다. 남자가 있으면 남자 자신만을 위한 것이 아닙니다. 남자가 있으면 여자가 있어야 합니다. 또 여자가 있으면 남자가 있어야 합니다. 주체와 대상 관계가 완전히 하나되는 기반을 통하여 가지고야 여기에 행복이 나오고, 이상이 나오고 발전이 나오는 것이지, 이 터전을 갖추지 않고는 무슨 행복이니 이상이니 발전이니 하는 것은 있을 수 없다는 것입니다.

그러면 행복은 어디서 나오느냐? 행복은 반드시 둘이 하나되는 데서 형성됩니다. 그건 여러분이 잘 알 것입니다. 그러면 둘이 하나되는 데 있어서 둘을 하나되게 하는 그것이 무엇이냐 할 때, 이것은 지식도 아니요, 권력도 아닙니다. 둘을 하나 만들 수 있는 그 힘이 무엇이냐? 이것이 사랑입니다. 사랑이라고 보는 것입니다. 그건 여러분이 부정할 수 없을 것입니다. 인생에 있어서 가장 귀한 것은 무엇이냐 할 때, ‘생명이지.’ 하겠지만 생명만 붙들어 가지고는 안 됩니다. 생명도 귀하지만 그 생명의 터전 위에 사랑을 결부시킬 수 있는 인연을 갖추어야 합니다. 그러지 않고는 그 생명도 오래 못 가서 없어지는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 인생에 있어서 가장 귀한 것은 무엇이냐? 생명보다도 사랑입니다.

그러면 사랑과 생명 중에 어떤 것이 먼저냐? 사랑이 먼저냐, 생명이 먼저냐 할 때, 여러분들은 생명이 먼저라고 생각할는지 모르겠지만 그것이 아니에요. 생명이 있기 전에 사랑, 사랑으로부터 생명이 시작되는 것입니다. 생명이 먼저가 아니라, 사랑이 먼저입니다. 이렇게 따지고 들어가면 이 우주의 생명체가 있느냐 없느냐 하는 문제를 생각하게 됩니다. 생명체가 있으면 좋겠다…. 그 생명체가 있어 가지고 이 우주를 형성했다면 그 생명체는 무엇으로 말미암아 시작되었느냐? 생명과 사랑을 중심삼고 볼 때에 반드시 사랑이 먼저라면…. 오늘날 인간들이 바라는 최고의 목적은 내가 생명의 가치를 존중시하는 것보다도, 사랑의 가치를 존중시할 수 있는 그런 자리에 도달하는 것입니다.

인간이 하나님의 최고의 대상
절대자가 계시다면 그 절대적인 하나님은 피조만물 가운데서 영물인 인간을 창조할 때, 인간의 생명이 그리워서 지은 것이 아닙니다. 그러면 인간을 왜 지었느냐? 주체만 가지고는 행복이 형성되지 않는 것입니다. 만일에 여기에 서 있는 선생님이 아무도 없는데 열렬히 이야기하게 된다면 저
ly wants to keep God within their own heart, where only they can see and know Him. This is the essence of human desire. 

In this context, where should God be? God should not be separated from us, neither placed in the east or west, nor above or below. He must be in one place with us. To achieve this, God must be the motive, and we must be the result; thus, the motive is within, and the result is outside. Therefore, God becomes the internal God, and humans become the external God.

This is the ideal foundation where humans can reside and where God and humans can live in a parent-child relationship. It is not that the father and son are two separate entities, but rather that they are one body. In other words, they become one unified being. This is not a hierarchical unity but a unity of inner and outer relationships. Within this relationship, there must be something that Adam and Eve, as well as their children, love the most. They desire to cherish that.

Isn't that true for you as well? When you have something you love the most, you hide it deep within. You do not throw away your beloved possessions on the street. The more precious the item, the more you want to keep it hidden. So, when it comes to God, who is the most precious to humanity, where should we keep Him? We cannot place Him on a high mountain or anywhere else. We want to keep Him close, always with us.

Moreover, human desire is such that if there is something I love, it must always be with me, and I wish that only I can see it while others cannot. If there is a loving God, I think, "That God is the one I love the most and is precious to me, so it would feel uncomfortable if others see Him. I want to keep Him in a place where only I can see and know Him!" Otherwise, I might lose Him or He could be taken away from me.

From this perspective, the desire of humans is to have God in a place where only they can see and know Him, within their own being. This is why the heart cannot be seen; the heart is invisible. But does that mean we do not know it? No, we know it more closely than anyone else. If we place God in our hearts, others cannot see Him. The only place where I can know, see, and cherish is within myself. Therefore, a person who loves God ideally wants to keep God within themselves.
The place where God can dwell is the center of the human heart. It concludes that there is no other place where He can reside. Therefore, God must dwell in our hearts, and we humans must be in a position similar to God's house. Thus, you should understand how happy it is that the heart is invisible.

When asking whether the heart is big enough for the absolute God who created this universe to live in, can a heart that is as small as a thatched house suffice? The heart is so vast that even if there are ten Gods, it wants to make them all its own. Isn't that true for your hearts? If there is something great, it wants to make it all its own. That is why there is nothing that cannot be placed before that heart. The heart can hold God and, if there are nations following that God, it wants to include those nations as well, or if there is a world, it wants to include that world too. That is how vast it is. Therefore, even when God is hosted in the heart, there is no accident. This is what the heart is.

Isn't your heart that big? It is to host God within that heart. God is a loving being and an absolute being, so one cannot place that being with absolute value elsewhere. Those who love want to go together, want to be together, and want to live together. Isn't that so? How do they want to live together? They want to delve into each other and become one. That is the essence of love.

Thus, in the relationship between the supreme ideal subject, God, and us humans, we cannot help but seek the connection to become one from the deep place in our hearts, which is why God must be in our hearts. This is undeniable.

What is the desire of humans after becoming the sons and daughters of God? Now, when looking at the bread on an equal level, if the father is a little better, it feels unpleasant, doesn't it? If there is something good, the father might hide it and say, "Hey, you must not see this. This is something I alone manage, and you must never touch it." This makes one feel bad. It is not trivial; it is a desire to have the best.

Because God loves His sons and daughters, it is the heart of a parent to want to give even what they do not have to their beloved children. If that obstruction becomes thicker, the action becomes duller. If it is made even thicker, it seems like there is no action. However, even if it seems like there is no action, it is still acting. Well, that’s good. South Korea is a country where it is hard to issue passports now; if you don’t get a plane ticket from abroad, you can’t leave the country. In a country like Japan, if I say over the phone right now to prepare 120 people to go to America, they will say "Yes" and prepare everything within a month.  
But look at South Korea. Even if you have prepared, they may not issue you a passport. Do you have a plane ticket? You need to show a round-trip ticket to get a passport. So, seeing that situation, I don’t want to do it. Therefore, it is best to just make Koreans suffer. (Laughter) This is not a laughing matter.  
Now, what will happen in just three years? We will create a global revival group. We will select global theologians. We will give those theologians checks for ten years at three times their annual salary. Do you understand? If we promise to give them ten years' worth of salary, any PhD in theology will fight to come out with a cane. This is how we will involve them. So, we will select about 20 people. We will give checks for ten years to global revivalists. The teacher has that much money. I still have money that I cannot use because the procedures in the United States are not completed; once the procedures are done, I will have an immense amount of money. The processing may take one year, three years, or ten years; we will have to wait and see, but this is the plan moving forward.  
Therefore, if we create a mobile corps by giving three times the current salary for ten years, do you think that will work? This time, I checked everything in America. You don’t even need three times; if you just give 1.5 times for ten years, everyone will be amazed and excited. This way, we will create global theologians and global revival speakers. Then, we will create mobile corps in each country with 1,000, 2,000, or 3,000 members. If we can create about 500, these revival groups will be overflowing wherever they go.  
When we held the World Victory Conference in Japan, when the Unification Church said, "Come together!" it was overflowing. Do you understand? About 3,000 people, that’s something you don’t even need to calculate. Do you understand? When we go around and say, "Hey, gather!" immediately, within three hours, 3,000 people will gather. Doesn’t that feel good? A global issue will arise where we can achieve great success wherever we go.  
These days, other revivalists are just following behind. There is only a dog following. Our revival group will create a global wind. When that happens, the theologians and pastors within that country will all be in a frenzy trying to invite international guests to their homes. This way, we will create a global theologians' association and a clergy association to take over everything. If established church pastors come, they might feel uncomfortable, but even if they do, there is nothing they can do. We must take over everything.  
Let’s see what happens to the pastors named here. Am I indebted to them, or are they indebted to me? I have not bowed my head and surrendered before them. But let’s see who surrenders. The spirit of this man who has been fighting until now has not died. If I am the leader, what are you? "Subordinates." Huh? The man who was chased around, Mr. Moon, has not died. Do you understand? You need to know that.  
Let’s conclude. Until today, for decades, through the long historical process of 20 years, the Unification Church has gone through numerous twists and turns. Sometimes in front of husbands, sometimes in front of brothers, sometimes in front of parents, they have endured all sorts of humiliation and betrayal.  
Oh, men and women of today who carry the sorrow of such an unjust history! As the day of final victory approaches us, we must unite completely.  
Thus, we must connect with the world and create a system where we can overcome the enemies of one nation, making them kneel and naturally submit before heaven. We must realize this and truly start from all of you in Seoul, reorganizing and uniting to present this movement on the front lines. This is the mission of the Unification Church members in Seoul that you must clearly understand.  
So, I hope to create a boom from here nationwide, and I hope you will respond well when it comes to future prescriptions. Do you understand? "Yes." Will you do it or not? "We will." Let’s see a show of hands from those who will do it! Put your hands down. Don’t just raise one hand; raise both hands! "Yes!" Let’s do it! "Let’s do it!" Let’s do it! "Let’s do it!" We must not lose to foreigners. Do you understand? "Yes."  
Then, knowing that, let me add that this time, I instructed the foreign members on two special things. One is, all responsibility for the mobile corps lies with those in the rear! The next is that every member of the Unification Church, including you and me, must buy 30 copies of the Principle book! This is an absolute command. You must buy 30 copies.  
Everyone must participate in the reading movement of the Principle.  
Since Unification Thought is based on living for others, it is not about buying books for oneself! That is exactly right. The more copies, the better. If you are to buy three copies, is it better to buy three or thirty? We, who are closest, must buy thirty copies, which is ten times three. Are you going to buy twelve copies? Twelve copies can only be shared among twelve people. Right? If you can only share among twelve people, then the tribe will disappear.  
Therefore, looking for a number that can exceed that, thirty copies is the best. In the sense of indemnifying Jesus' 30 years of life, and in the sense of indemnifying the three days, we aim to create a global movement for total indemnification centered around the number three, asking each person to buy thirty copies of the book for thirty people. Do you understand? "Yes." Now, the Unification Church members have been told that everyone in the world must buy thirty copies, but is there any exception for Korea? "No." Is there anyone who thinks there could be an exception? No. Then everyone must do it. So, you must buy thirty copies. Now, let’s see a show of hands from those who will buy thirty copies. "30,000 copies." So, we sold 30,000 copies. (Laughter) How much is the Unification Church Principle book? It’s 800 won, so how much is that in total? 24 million won. It’s easy to make money, right? Yes, I will make money and share it with you instead of keeping it for myself. Do you understand? But I shouldn’t give it to you; according to the principle of restoration through indemnity, I will share it with the people of South Korea.  
Then, the Unification Church members should think, "Oh, rather than keeping it for ourselves, we should share it with the people of South Korea." This is the spirit and lifestyle of Unification Church members. Therefore, through the teacher, we should say, "Let’s give for the nation rather than for ourselves. Let’s give for the world rather than for the nation." This is the main thought of Unification Thought. Therefore, the money from selling the books will be used for the nation! Does that feel good or bad? "Good."

The conclusion is that it must be paid within 40 days. Since we cannot publish the books within 40 days, it must be paid by the time they are published. We cannot buy them because they are not published; when they are published, everyone will compete to buy them. This will be recorded in history. In the future, it will be recorded which of your ancestors was ranked where. Isn’t that amazing? It’s not that Teacher Moon is smart and organized it that way. It is destined to happen that way. Do you understand?  
So, what do we do with the thirty copies? We distribute them to thirty people. Buying thirty copies means distributing them to thirty people, giving one copy to each person once a month. You lend one copy for a month. To how many people? To one person? With one copy, if you hold it for two weeks, you can lend it to two people, and if you read it in one week, you can lend it to four people in a month. So, at the very least, you lend one copy to one person each month. Then, in a year, with 365 days, one person will lend the book to 360 people. If we conduct the lending movement every two weeks, 720 people will read the book in a year. Do you understand?  
Do the members of the Principle Study Group understand? If there are just ten members in the Principle Study Group at Seoul National University, how many people will have read the book after a year? How many? What do you mean a few hundred? It’s 3,600. If there are thirty people, how many is that? If thirty people engage in the book distribution movement, it will conclude that there is no one who has not read the Unification Church Principle. This is a powerful strategy.  
Then, can’t we lend a book to one person each day and retrieve it from one person? Anyone who says they can’t do this should not even call themselves a member of the Unification Church. Can you do it or not? Can you do it or not? "We will." Let’s see a show of hands from those who will do it. Put your hands down! Now, we will do it as a command. Since we have made all the promises….  
Effective ways to utilize the Principle  
So, we have launched this movement globally. For example, if there are ten thousand Unification Church members, how many people can we distribute books to in a year? If there are ten thousand members in a year, that’s 360 times, right? So, 3.6 million people will read the book.
Yes. Isn't that right? Am I wrong? If we lend books once every two weeks, that means 7.2 million people will read them. That is why the Communist Party has expanded its influence globally, not by people walking around, but by using books. Do you understand?

Also, in terms of evangelism, people who join the Unification Church after reading books are more useful than those who join after attending lectures. That is why the teacher has said to write the principles of the Unification Church as difficult as possible. Ordinary people need to come in... What the Unification Church is looking for now is leaders. We need one person to lead, not a thousand people to follow. Do you understand? "Yes."

So if you give books to 360 people, how many do you think will be evangelized among them? Look. Right now in Japan, 20% of people who hear the principles become members. If 100 people hear the teachings, 20 will become members. This is because the level of knowledge is high. In Korea, the level is low... Still, those people have a high level of knowledge, and the higher the level, the higher the ratio becomes. Do you understand? If world-class professors hear the teachings, more than half of them will support it. This is how it works. The higher the level of knowledge, the higher the ratio becomes. This is how it is meant to be. Do you understand? Therefore, the low ratio in Korea is due to the low level of knowledge. No matter how low the level is, it should be at least 2% to 3%...

For example, we have the Korea-America Cultural Freedom Foundation in the United States, which sends out 100,000 letters nationwide every month. Sometimes they send out up to 1 million letters. In those letters, they say, "Our organization is like this, and if you have a heart for it, please donate." The response rate is usually around 2% to 4%. Generally, it is set at over 2%. Do you understand? If you send a piece of mail to someone you haven't seen or met and ask for donations, the number of people donating can reach up to 4%. At the very least, it will be over 2%.

Considering this, if you sincerely go out and lend books to 360 people and put in effort, what percentage do you think will be evangelized? Even if it's 2%, that means seven people will be evangelized in a year. If it's 3%, more than 10 people will be evangelized. If you lend books every two weeks, how many will that be? You could evangelize more than 15 to 20 people. Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, the conclusion is that there is no problem in evangelizing one person a month.

That is why we are conducting this movement globally, where each person evangelizes more than one person a month. It will happen automatically. And if people who have read the books have questions, they should hold a gathering. If there are people who want to know more and think the teachings are good, they should not keep it to themselves but introduce it to their wives, relatives, siblings, or even distant relatives. They should say, "I will explain this to you, so you take the lead." If only 10 people come, you could evangelize 100 people. Do you understand? This is how evangelism should be done.

So from now on, you must engage in evangelistic activities with this book. Do you understand? Until now, we have a responsibility to inform the entire nation and the world, regardless of who you are... Those who understand the purpose and hear the teachings will be blessed. Until now, we have opened the doors to the north, south, east, and west publicly, even breaking down the walls. But now we will build the walls and only open the doors to draw in those who are needed, centered around this booklet as the method of evangelism. Do you understand? A vast movement will unfold. If it reaches a million people, how much is that? 360 times that is 360 million people. I have proposed this movement; will you participate in it or not? "We will."

Everyone has promised to participate, so there is no need to ask again. However, because I cannot trust the Korean people, I will ask once more. I have been deceived so much that I wonder if I should ask again. You said, "Birth, growth, completion," so will you participate in this? "Yes, we will." Is this sincere, is it a family matter? "It is sincere." If your bones are trembling, then it is sincere, right? "Yes." You must decide with a trembling heart; otherwise, I cannot trust you.

Because I feel sorry for you, the Unification Church principle book is 800 won, but I will give it to you at cost. So did we sell it for 400 won before? We will distribute it all for 400 won. Do you understand? "Yes." If you cannot do even this, there will be no forgiveness. Moreover, young men and women will be caught up in the blessing issue immediately. (Laughter) They will be caught up right away. If you don't do it for three years, you cannot. You must do it for three years, to the point where your feet have holes...

I have even gone boar hunting in Gangwon Province. I thought, "I need to do something to lead these Unification Church members around." I think it would be good to do it again this time. Wouldn't it be good to try it?

Would you prefer me to push from behind or pull from the front? Would you prefer to be pulled by the nose from the front, or would you prefer to be whipped from behind? Which one? Either one would be suitable, so how should we do it? Should I pull from the front, or push from behind? "Push from behind." (Laughter) You want me to push from behind? What if I just leave you alone? Is it better to leave you alone or to push? "It is better to leave you alone." Even if I leave you alone, if you go faster than being pushed, then I will leave you alone! (Laughter)

Then what will you do after I leave you alone? I will have to go abroad now. This October, there will be a World Scientists Conference in the United States. So I will select two of the most authoritative people from Korea to go. I have instructed to select people from Japan as well. When we hold seminars centered around 10 countries, the important keynote speech must be given by Teacher Moon. Do you understand? That is why I cannot miss October.

Now is the time to act for world missions.

So I have spent all the overall expenses. Since South Korea does not believe, I think we need to educate these people a bit. Do you understand? Therefore, in March of next year, I plan to gather global business leaders. We are gradually moving forward. Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, for Teacher to operate on such a global stage, it is necessary to pass through South Korea. There are at least two years left.

I feel a responsibility to protect this country until Kim Il-sung celebrates his sixtieth birthday, so I have been praying fervently. From now on, we will extend... Originally, the prayer period was supposed to start this May. Isn't that right? From now on, we will be praying. We must pray until this October, extending it by three years. We will enter a six-month prayer period again. From May to June, July, August, September, and October, that is six months. Until the three-year period is over, during that time, either Kim Il-sung will die, or some wind will blow. Do you understand? We have three years left to hold onto this nation, hold onto the world's communist realm, and pray centered on God. Do you understand? "Yes." 

Because of such urgent issues, we must establish our global activity base... This fall, we will create mobile units in more than 10 countries. So Teacher must manage it directly. Therefore, I am planning to contract for a one-year airplane ticket. I will need to travel around like this. So I will not be able to stay long in the country. I was born as a son of this Republic of Korea and have shown patriotism that is not inferior to anyone in this country. I have given my loyalty that would not be embarrassing even to patriots. My responsibility is now complete.

After extending for two years and finishing the second seven-year course, those who have worked hard will all become global figures. They will all go to the United States and create mobile units that can lead advanced countries in Europe. You must understand that there is a responsibility to create supervisory personnel. The Unification Church has prepared a global stage, and the foundation of that Unification Church is... Just a little further, young people who graduated from Seoul National University will come in fighting and lining up. At that time, there may come a time when they will not select anyone without going through a test of hundreds to one. Just wait and see if that will happen.

And by 1975, our Unification Church must establish mission departments in 120 countries. If that happens, it will be difficult to meet Teacher. Even if I leave Korea and stay in one country for a month and then come back, how many years will it take? It will take 10 years. Yes, will they let me stay for just a month after seeing Teacher in that country? "Please stay for just three months." If that happens, it will take 30 years. Right now, we are boldly starting to go global. But when that time comes, it will mean returning with a cane after turning 80. (Laughter) This is not a joke. Soon, representatives from each country will flock to their home countries. I will have the responsibility to handle the affairs for those people, so there will come a time when I will not have time to meet you.

So I had planned to build over 120 floors on the land of Yeouido, but because the ground is weak, I am now planning to build up to 70 floors or more. At that time, ambassadors from all countries will come there and say, "Teacher, please give us orders," and a movement will unfold to spread it worldwide. At that time, people will say, "Oh, why couldn't I join the Unification Church? That guy was behind me, but he became like this after joining the Unification Church!" They will drool and cry, but they will realize that there will come a time when they cannot join. This is not a joke. Do you understand? 

In the 1960s, I told you, "Let's wait for 10 years! After 7 years, it will be like this. Just wait for 10 years." I never dreamed it would turn out like this. Do you understand? Even if I go to the United States and confront the best in the seven major cities, they will not be able to say a word. I am not just talking nonsense; I will speak in a way that fits the theory and resolve it. Looking back this time, the world seems ridiculous. The global mobile units are being told to do just that.

Just as I cannot speak all the languages of each country and need interpreters, you can do it in your own language, so anyone can participate in this movement. Young people will do it. Will you do it or not? Everyone will blow the election trumpet. In the future, when election time comes in the United States, we will create experts who can blow the trumpet. Because we are in a position where we must protect America before heaven in defending the free world, we must quickly establish a global activity base centered on America. This is why you must take responsibility for Korea in the future. Do you understand? "Yes." Occasionally, there may be guests...

Everyone must go through mobile unit activities.

So, should Korea recover quickly, or should America recover quickly? Korea has done enough; it can be left alone. If we try to do more, we will suffer a lot. Do you understand? If there is a fight, we must fight at the forefront with Kim Il-sung. If we fight at the 38th parallel, Unification Church members must be at the front line of the 38th parallel. Do you understand? "Yes." Therefore, we must not cause any damage... If we turn the front line to America, we do not need to fight at the 38th parallel. Do you understand? That is why we must connect such operations, and this is what the third global tour is for. Do you understand? Know that you should not be ashamed before the global times.

So, after three years, this mobile unit will organize revival teams, and when we gather these revival teams, we will charter a jumbo airplane that can carry at least 480 people for twelve months a year. I have already looked into it. We can even buy a plane and send it to Korean Air to travel the world. I have already checked everything.

Then, we will extract excellent mobile units from each country. The men selected at this time will be numerous. The women will also be numerous. Those women will marry global Unification Church men, and those men will marry global Unification Church women. Do you agree? Those who participate will have to speak English, French, and Spanish because it will be on a global stage. You must be proficient in all three languages. Do you understand? This will definitely happen within three years. Those who can only speak English will only need a year and a half, and if they work hard, they can learn French and Spanish in just one year.

All of that foundation... If I just sign, you can go to France and live for 10 years. Do you understand? Even if you have no money, when you go to France, if I sign and say, "I am sending this man because he will be needed in the future, so you must feed him and educate him for 10 years!" they will have to educate him. Do you understand? The same goes for Spain, and the time will come when this will be possible in every country. At that time, if you only know English, you will be sent to that country, and both men and women will learn the language within a year, even if it requires rigorous training.

So, you will learn in France and in Spain. We will create a global mobile unit movement. This is Teacher's plan. Therefore, we are currently organizing the mobile unit members who are being trained in each country. Do you understand? This is not a lie. Teacher Moon of the Unification Church does not lie in public. It will definitely happen. I will earn the money to fund it. Teacher can earn money quite well. Do you understand? "Yes."
