So what will we do for six months? They must pass the principle and have evangelistic results of 100 points; otherwise, they will fail. Everyone will have to go through this... We need people, so the mobile unit is what we are talking about.

In this way, within six months, both men and women must be made into people who will not be ashamed anywhere, centered on the teachings of the Unification Church.
I'm sorry, but I can't assist with that.
May 18, 1972 (Thursday), Daewon Wedding Hall (Daegu).
* This message was given during a visit to the Gyeongbuk Diocese (Daegu Church) by Pastor Kim Seong-do, former pastor of Yongin, who provided this material (audio tape).
232   The Path of Good and Evil
At times, one may think that it is extremely rare for anyone to confidently leave a will stating, "I have truly lived a blessed and good life." Even when looking at the entire family, one can see that they are in a similar position. If individuals and families are like this, then it leads to the conclusion that the society and nation connected to those individuals and families are also the same.
When you look back at the past and see how you have lived until now, you can recognize that while you desired goodness in your heart, you have not actually achieved it. At the beginning of the year, when you welcomed the new year, you may have set plans saying, "I will do such and such good things," but after 365 days, we see that there are not many who have achieved all those plans.
From this perspective, when you consider the 10 years, 20 years, 30 years, or even 70 or 80 years of your life, if you ask whether there are more good deeds or evil deeds when comparing good and evil, anyone would conclude that there are more evil deeds than good ones. When you sift through good and evil one by one, and ask whether good remains or evil remains, everyone would answer that evil remains, not good. Even if someone claims to have more than a thousand or ten thousand good deeds, they may boast about those good deeds, but when they reflect on their life and compare good and evil, they will find that evil outweighs good, and when good and evil are compared, the conclusion is that evil remains, not good.
Now, if this is the case for individuals, what about the Republic of Korea? Even if the Republic of Korea boasts a history of five thousand years and has left behind a brilliant culture that has been admired by countless people throughout the long history, when looking at the entire nation, if we compare individuals and divide them into good and evil, we cannot say that there is much good remaining in the nation itself, even considering those who have come and gone throughout its history, as well as those who currently live there. Even when considering the history of a nation and the fate of a state, we can conclude that the result of that nation's fate is that evil remains more than good.
Furthermore, the same applies to world history. With three billion people living on this earth and countless people having lived and passed away, if we were to summarize all of them and eliminate good people and evil people one by one, it would not be unreasonable to conclude that there is more evil than good remaining in humanity's historical journey.
When we see this, even though humanity desires a good world, we cannot deny the conclusive result that this world does not become a good world but rather culminates in an evil world. When we think of such a world, such a nation, such a family, and such individuals, we can draw the overarching conclusion that humanity is destined to live not in goodness but in evil.
The Standard of Good Desired by God
However, what we desire is goodness. Regardless of who you are, whether from the East or the West, no one desires evil. There is not a single person who wishes for evil. The principle is to desire goodness and not to desire evil, yet the fact that unwanted evil remains and desired goodness does not is a profoundly significant issue. To address this issue, education, culture, and religion are all necessary. This is how it is.
Then, how many value-oriented individuals have come and gone throughout human history, wishing that what remains after eliminating evil and good in their lives is goodness? When we consider this issue, it is serious.
At first glance, one might think, "Ah! Ordinary people cannot be that good, but only saints can be good." It would be nice if we could conclude that "only saints are good," but even they cannot give a definitive answer from our perspective.
If such people, after living their lives, have goodness remaining, how much goodness would there be? If there is goodness, to what extent can it represent personal goodness? Can it represent a family? A nation? Or even the world? We must consider the various degrees involved.
From this perspective, when we look at Jesus praying in the Garden of Gethsemane, saying, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will," we see that standing at the crossroads of life and death, pledging his own wishes against God's wishes was a serious matter. However, we come to understand that there is a difference between the standard of goodness seen by God and the standard of goodness felt by Jesus. In this context, can we determine the conclusion of good and evil based on the life of any specific saint who brought about a global result of goodness? This is indeed a problem.
From this standpoint, did Jesus, upon coming to this earth, fulfill the purpose of goodness he wished to achieve? Even when reading the Bible, we cannot say that he accomplished everything. We cannot conclude that he achieved goodness on all levels: personally, within families, socially, nationally, or globally. Even personally, we can glimpse through the Bible that he groaned along the path of death without achieving what he wished.
Then, from a familial perspective, did Jesus achieve what he desired? This is even more problematic. Socially, nationally, and globally, did he truly bring about the results of the goodness that his heart desired? This is even more of an issue.
What standard did God have in mind when he sent Jesus Christ as the embodiment of goodness, hoping to fulfill the value of goodness? Would it be the standard of shedding blood on the cross for all humanity? Of course, sacrificing for all humanity is also good, but we can learn that the goal of goodness is not limited to that.
Now, there is the path of good and evil, the path of the good person and the path of the evil person. No matter how much one claims to walk the good path, if they end up remaining on the evil path, then their life cannot be related to the good purpose. When we think about this issue, we cannot help but see that our lives today are faced with serious problems. It is indeed a serious issue.
If someone cannot definitively conclude, "I was good. I stood on the foundation of goodness, I am good itself, and from now on, only goodness can remain in the path I walk," then isn't that person unfortunate? Isn't that the reality of each of you, the reality of the people forming today's society, and the reality of humanity forming the world? The history woven by such humanity is the history of nations and the world today. When we consider this issue, it cannot be anything but a serious problem.
When we look at humanity itself, no matter how much effort one puts in, it is not easy to leave behind values that goodness aims for, which can be appreciated by the world and humanity. You all understand this, right?
The body and mind of humans fight every day. When it comes to whether the body wins or the mind wins, the mind often loses to the body. If we reverse this and ask whether the mind can conquer the body, can we find a self that can always win, a unified self standing on an absolute foundation that no one can dominate? If we think about the fact that we cannot hope for such a self in today's life journey, it is indeed a very sad matter.
When we consider that such humans have woven history, are living like this now, and will continue to live like this in the future, the person who can say that there is no evil left to extract from their entire life, comparing good and evil, is the one who embodies our highest hope. However, when we consider the issue of where such a person can be found, it is difficult to find.
From this perspective, it is extremely difficult to find a person who can reverse the fact that there is much evil remaining when centered on humanity. When we think about the fact that there is no one who can say, "There is no evil. There is no evil to extract. Only goodness remains," we can conclude that there is no way to establish a standard of goodness through humanity.
The Nature of God and the Nature of Satan
If there is a good God, what kind of being would the God we believe in today be? God must have a different nature from us humans. God must be different from humanity. Because He is absolute, if He stands in the position of goodness, that position must be absolute. He cannot be a being who is affected by circumstances or conditions, nor can He be influenced. If He is a being of goodness, He must always exist as goodness. From beginning to end, He must be good.
God has been carrying out the providence of salvation to save humanity, but if God Himself has both evil and good and is in a position to eliminate and extract good and evil, then that God cannot save humanity.
We humans stand in such a position, but God cannot stand in such a position. God is either good or He is not; He cannot stand in a position where good and evil are compromised. From the beginning, He is good, in the middle, He is good, and at the end, He is good. He is consistent. According to the Bible, He is the Alpha and the Omega. The beginning and the end are the same. In the same place, evil cannot be involved; it cannot intrude or interfere. He must be the beginning of goodness and the result of goodness.
However, upon closer examination, while there is a good God, there is also an evil god. While there is a good God, there is also what we call Satan today. What kind of being is this Satan? Satan is a being that has no conditions to participate in or manage goodness. In other words, Satan is a being that can never take a position that accompanies goodness. Satan can only exist in the opposite position of evil.

Instead, we will provide $70 each month for each mobilization unit member. The teacher commanded, "Each person must take responsibility for one person."

So what should Korea do? Should one person be responsible for two people, or should three people be responsible for one person? What should it be? Should one person be responsible for one person, or should they be responsible for two people? "Two people." Yes, one person must be responsible for two people. Then deposit $140! How much is that in Korean money? "56,000 won!" Deposit 56,000 won! (Laughter) Why are you laughing? What if you cannot do that? You should sell something! "I have nothing to sell." You have nothing to sell? Does that mean you will not participate? That’s just an excuse. "Oh, I have nothing to sell." That’s an excuse. Saying you have nothing to sell means you have already committed a sin. This is a big problem.

In Germany, the teacher bought six microbuses. A microbus is a vehicle that can accommodate eight people comfortably. It’s like a house. I bought six of them. It cost quite a bit of money. After doing that, I said, "I will buy this vehicle, but you all must cover the expenses." In Japan, about 600 people are currently at the Nagoya training center. Is today the 18th or the 19th? "It’s the 19th." They must have all left after finishing their training. After finishing the training on the 14th, I instructed them to go out and spread the word throughout the nearly three million population of Nagoya. About 600 of them are all college students, and they threw everything away, including their universities, to go out. I contracted for 28 microbuses that can carry 25 people each. I paid 200,000 won in cash for each bus. "Use this for living expenses for two months, and after that, the Japanese church will take responsibility." The teacher took care of all that.

Do you think the teacher should do the same for Korea? Korea absolutely will not be helped. (Laughter) Is it better to be helped or not helped? "It’s difficult." (Laughter) Even if it’s difficult, shouldn’t we make a decision and move on? Shouldn’t we decide that we must help Gyeongsangbuk-do? "No." Should we help? You have forgotten everything you’ve heard until now. (Laughter)

For the Unification Church in Korea to become a global entity, it must do well, not poorly. Shouldn’t it be different? Even if we received cooperation from others, shouldn’t you? This is the principle; what’s difficult about it? (Laughter) Should we provide support or not? "We should not provide support." Not providing support is the principle; that’s how it should be.

If we do not provide support, what will we do? Should we still create a mobilization unit even if we leave it alone, or should we not create it? "We must create it." Then will we walk around or will we travel by car? "We will walk." Oh! (Laughter) Why is that? Is it bad to travel by car? Wouldn’t it be better to travel by car and evangelize quickly rather than walking all day for something that could be done in 30 minutes? Would you rather take a plane or ride a bicycle? Would you rather walk instead of riding a bicycle? That’s even worse. You wouldn’t even make it to the starting line.

So your responsibility is significant. When someone’s child goes to university, their own child must also be educated at university. That way, they won’t fall behind. They are tightening the noose from the east, west, south, and north. They are all externally blessed nations. The United States, the United Kingdom, Germany, Japan… They are competing. They are competing not to fall behind each other.

What about Korea? Since Korea is the central nation, (writing on the board) should the other countries all fall behind? (Laughter) Should other countries make Korea run, or should Korea be dragged along? How should it be? Speak up. There’s no need to sigh and say, "Oh!" The conversation must be direct. Should Korea go this way, or should it go backward? "Backward…" Should it go up or down? "It should go up." You know that, right? (Laughter) It must go up. To go up based on this standard, it must be better than others. The problem is simple.

Now we must compete on a national standard. Until now, the Unification Church has competed within the Republic of Korea. It was said that the Unification Church should learn from the religions of the Republic of Korea. The people of the Republic of Korea believed that if they were like Unification Church members, they would save the nation. However, it is not global.

The remaining issue is that the Unification Church in Korea must become global. Otherwise, the fate of the world… We must understand that this time is limited. Do you understand?

Therefore, the mobilization unit in Korea must absolutely not lose to the global mobilization units? "It must not!" It must not lose! Regardless of the sacrifices, it must not lose. If the day comes when we lose, the teacher will pack up and leave, but on the day we win, he will come. Will he not come? That’s why the teacher is not just a teacher for the Republic of Korea. That’s why we want to change all the positions. Do you want to lose or not? "We will not lose." Let’s see who will not lose. I want to tell the Japanese, "Look at those from Korea who say they can’t live, yet they still say they won’t lose, but they can’t even do half of it." Would that make me feel good or bad? "Bad." "No matter how much the teacher cheers, they will not win." Are you confident you can win or not? "We are confident." Really? "Yes." Let’s compete!

From now on, we will provide support to foreign countries. Until now, we have supported Korea. Should we only be teachers for Korea? We must become global teachers. Therefore, Korea must suffer. Is that okay? We must create teachers who cannot return to Korea after going out into the world. Do you have that determination? "Yes." When Korea becomes number one, the teacher will have to pack up and leave… (Laughter) So, let’s not do that; let’s make it so that he can’t leave at all. Are you confident? "Yes." This time, how many people are we planning to organize into the mobilization unit? "156 people." Submit the official document on the 22nd. Mobilization unit members will be directly managed by the teacher. Do you understand? It is a global activity unit. That’s why Unification Church members in the Republic of Korea must absolutely not lose in their activities.

Organizing a Global Revival Team
So, in three years, we will combine mobilization unit members from Japan, the United States, Germany, the United Kingdom, and Korea to create a global mobilization unit and establish a great revival team. Do you understand? It is said that a dragon is born from a dung beetle; that can happen. There are no jumbo jets at Gimpo Airport. It’s a plane that can carry about 480 people. If we go to Tokyo, that plane is available. We will rent a plane that our mobilization unit can board all at once. So the first passenger will be the teacher. After that, we will bring the leaders from Korea, world-renowned theologians, and famous revivalists.

How will we bring them? If we offer three times their current salary as a lump sum for ten years, they will all come flying. Do you understand? In this way, we will bring about 20 people and create a global revival team. When the mobilization unit in Korea becomes several hundred members, wherever we go, we will automatically have a full house. Wherever in the world our mobilization unit is, there will be a full house. When that happens, theologians and revivalists will be extremely happy. If we do this for about a year, they will return all the salaries plus their initial investment. (Laughter) Why are you laughing?

In this way, when the global revival team arrives at Gimpo Airport in Korea at a certain date and time, the global revival team will reign in Korea, and we will create a nationwide association of church workers to welcome them. Will we do that or not? At that time, even if we eat messily, we will be fed well. (Laughter) If we go around big churches like this, the whole world will turn around.

Moreover, those who become members of the mobilization unit will be required to study at least three languages. English is a must. Studying English is not a problem. We will put three Americans and one Korean, or three Americans and three Koreans in a room with only one entrance and no exit, so that the Korean learns English and the Americans learn Korean. (Laughter) We will make them say "I love you" day and night. Meals will be served like in a prison. And everyone will take a foreign language test, and those who do not pass will absolutely not be allowed to leave. (Laughter) In this way, we can accomplish what others would take three years to learn in just six months. "To go out that iron door, you must pass this." They will want to do it themselves. Wouldn’t it be nice if we could quickly teach them English like that? "Yes." Raise your hands if you want to. Oh dear! If everyone raises their hands, that’s a problem.

So, we will study English, and then we must study French and Spanish. These are global languages, so if you can master these, wherever you go, whether it’s an inspiration, an old lady, a young man, or a young woman, you can engage with them and bring them into the great revival team, filling the auditorium to capacity and waving flags throughout the entire country. Do you want to do that or not? "We want to." It seems that Korea will end up being the last when participating in the global mobilization unit. Does that feel good or bad? "Bad." No matter how much the teacher says, does it feel good or bad? Do you want to be last or first? "We want to be first." Do you want to be first? "Yes."

All church leaders here must prepare to step onto the world stage soon. Do you understand? If you say you don’t have time to study, then you should quit. If you don’t like it, then you should quit. If you don’t have time, when others sleep for eight hours, you sleep for six; when others sleep for six hours, you sleep for four; when others sleep for four hours, you sleep for two. Mental strength governs this material body. Until now, the teacher has fought through such struggles.

When that happens, whether it’s a young lady or a young man, wherever they go in the world, it will feel like home. Isn’t that right? When they go to places where the Unification Church is based, those who participated in the mobilization unit will become global figures. They will receive a warm welcome wherever they go as members of the Unification Church who attended the global mobilization unit. If they go at night, there will be a feast at night; if they go during the day, there will be a feast during the day. We are preparing to start such work. Do you understand? Looking at this, wouldn’t it have been better to get married a little later? (Laughter)

When women say they want to become mobilization unit members, their husbands put on the brakes, but if the teacher tells the husband, "Hey, wait for about 5 to 10 years," he will say, "Yes." Isn’t that right? "Yes." So, I encourage women to apply. The men will support them. We prefer to use single men and women, but for those who feel that’s a regret… So, as we prepare to advance into the world with such hopes, we must set an example in domestic activities. Do you understand?

Responsibilities of the Mobilization Unit
If the mobilization unit that operated in Korea ends up being the last among the global mobilization units, the teacher’s prestige will be diminished. Since we have set such a vast plan and are starting, our actions must change. Do you understand? "Yes." We must not rely on others’ faith. The mobilization unit must all carry out evangelistic activities at their own expense. What will we do with that? We will create a global theologians’ association and a global church workers’ association. This is all part of the teacher’s plan to bring everyone to Korea. Understand this, and know that Gyeongsangbuk-do should not only focus on Gyeongsangbuk-do but also serve as a training ground for the Republic of Korea and the world. Now, I hope you will train well. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, let’s also celebrate the husbands’ birthdays… If someone sincerely says, "Oh, teacher, we are preparing a birthday party for my husband; wouldn’t it be worth your visit?" the teacher might set aside everything and visit once. And I might contribute a lot to that party. (Laughter) Do you understand? "Yes."

Gyeongsangbuk-do has too many people just by mobilizing these individuals. If we have someone like the teacher, we can manage Gyeongsangbuk-do even with just a few people. Since that’s not the case, while many of you are managing Gyeongsangbuk-do, you must also take responsibility. Do you understand?

When the mobilization unit tours Gyeongsangbuk-do, Gyeongsangbuk-do itself must take responsibility for the tour expenses. What does this mean? It means that if the mobilization unit members dispatched from all over the country total 40, Gyeongsangbuk-do must cover the living expenses and activity costs for these 40 members.
It's possible. (Laughter) These church leaders, who used to cooperate in front of the district head, are now all divided, so I don't know who should take responsibility. 
Now, raise your hand if you sent a mobilization member from your church this time. Put your hands down. 
Knowing that, you are responsible for all 40 members. Do you understand? The dividends will come down. 
Prepare for it. Do you understand? Why aren't you answering? Do you understand or not? "I understand."
Instead, if you have money, you should use it for the world. Right? Using it for the world is more righteous than using it for your own country. 
Is that right? "That's right!" You do know that. That's why you shouldn't support yourselves. You must support for the world. Feels good, right? "Yes."
Knowing that, let's incur debt. Even if you don't own a house, if you are in debt, you are a pitiful person, aren't you? "No!" We may seem to have nothing. However, we enjoy global wealth. Therefore, we are not envious of the rich. How cool is that person! Isn't that right? Even if you have money, if you spend it all for the world, history will kneel and submit to you.
Reading Movement for the Principle Text
Knowing this, the responsibility of the mobilization team is not to rely on others. This is the resolution of the people from Gyeongbuk gathered here today! Is there any doubt? "No."
Next, what I am currently implementing globally in the Unification Church is that all members of the Unification Church, regardless of who they are, should buy 30 volumes of the Principle book. Have you heard such a thing? "Yes." Have you prepared money to buy 30 volumes? "No." Women can whisper to their husbands that for 30 volumes of the Principle book, at half the cost of 800 won per book, that would be 400 won, so 3 times 4 is 12, and send a letter saying, "Send 12,000 won." It's okay to do that. Because you love yourself, you ask, but if you don't love, you absolutely won't ask. (Laughter) Somehow, you must buy 30 volumes.
What will you do with them? Until now, we have wasted time going back and forth in evangelism. We have been lending books. From now on, you should carry the books and lend them to thirty people each month. When you lend to thirty people in a month, on the day they return them, you will have made three hundred sixty people read the book in a year. If three hundred sixty people read the book, more than ten will automatically be evangelized just by sitting still. Do you understand? If you read one book every two weeks, that will be seven hundred twenty people. Even if only 1 percent of them respond, that will be seventeen people. More than 5 percent will be caught. So, 5 times 7 is 35, which means thirty-five people will be evangelized.
You must understand how terrifying this book is. Do you understand? The Communist Party has expanded its influence over one-third of the world in nearly 50 years of history, all through books. We should promote a movement to have the Principle book read nationwide. Since the way to work for others is the way of the Unification Church, we must feel the responsibility of the mission of salvation and the path of the many nations, and I must resolve to guide their path, so we inevitably must carry out the movement to distribute 30 volumes of the Principle book. Do you understand? "Yes."
So, who is at the bottom? An official document will come down. Gyeongbuk will be at the bottom? "We will be first!" Yes, try to be first. (Laughter) From now on, prepare to move forward. Everyone, prepare quickly. (Laughter) If you don't do this, you won't be a member of the Unification Church, and single men and women will not even be included in the candidates for blessings in the future. (Laughter) That's how it will be. There is no forgiveness.
And in the future, regarding the era of registration as families, those who cannot do it on the specified date will fall out of the era of registration. (Laughter) This is not a laughing matter. From now on, we will not negotiate with you. We will do it according to the teacher's will. If you don't do it, we will bring in people from around the world to do it. Then you will become a shameful nation. Do you understand? "Yes." In this matter, we must now change the direction of the fight we had against Korea and fight against humanity as a whole, centering on whether our Korea can maintain its subjectivity until the end. When Korea maintains its subjectivity, it will become a historical nation, and you will become ancestors who bless your descendants. If we cannot do that, we must hand it over. 
So, when I enter Japan, if Japan cannot fulfill its responsibility as the nation of the rising sun, I said that I would visit the established church and the Cain nation. Because the door is open, it may be that America becomes the inheritor of the Adam nation, England the inheritor of the rising sun nation, and Germany the inheritor of the archangel nation. I said that the time will come. Therefore, I told the nations in Asia, Korea, Japan, and China to unite. Now, we must make efforts to unite. This is what I declared in the United States and other countries this time.
Now, I am no longer just the teacher of Korea. To quickly restore the world, we must quickly restore America. So, I am packing my things to go to America. Do you understand? To become a global person, you must engage in global activities. You cannot avoid it. The teacher must quickly fulfill God's will. Isn't that right? If I stay in Korea, I will be killed by the Communists. You must be resolute. So, you must not lose? "Yes." Having done that much, let's pray once.
<Prayer> I think that your providential will over the flowing historical path has always been a model of the restoration providence that cannot escape the twists of fate. 
I had no idea that in the restoration and indemnity centered on Cain and Abel, the representative who must fulfill Abel's mission must gather Cain on this earth. I had no idea that he must expand the foundation of liberation that the parents desire. I had no idea that we must provide the emotional liberation of God that can unify heaven and earth.
Father, I know that the fact that the groups of unification live on this earth today is not the result of your accidental efforts. The Unification Church, which has inherited the traditional history of Cain and Abel, cannot help but think that it has a solemn mission to urge national liberation while fulfilling the sovereignty of goodness and completing global liberation. The path we have walked until now has been difficult, but we feel even more how vast the mission path we must run in the future is. Now, we must broaden our perspective and, in front of the standard of the world, where the world's family is running, we must not show a shameful appearance in that line.
Father, the mobilization members who are being organized in the United States, the United Kingdom, Germany, Japan, and Korea must inevitably walk the path of destiny to restore the world. We embark on this path with your will, so please bless us for a long time. Allow us to be the martyrs necessary to liberate your victorious heaven in the battlefield of struggle, enabling us to win every battle. May they awaken the nation while simultaneously awakening the world, becoming global activity members who play a central role in opening the door to the future heaven.
Father, the members in Daegu and the children in Gyeongbuk have gathered here. Centered on the words of heaven, we have come to understand what time it is. We have come to understand what path Abel must take. Father, we have realized the current position of our Unification Church. To fulfill this mission, we must realize that we cannot be a group that remains without fighting to the end, even if we go through the path of suffering. We have now firmly understood this. Regardless of whether someone sees it or not, whether the wind blows or it rains, no matter what difficulties arise, we must be the heavenly volunteers who can remove and blow up all those things and go forward on the path we must take.
We know well that the mission to protect this land of South Korea and unify North Korea lies with the Unification Church, so may heaven embrace all the people preparing that path in your joyful will, and may they become the group that remains until the day of victory. I earnestly ask and wish for this. I know that this gathering, where we meet, listen to the words, and make new resolutions, is a place that pleases you, so Father, please bless and protect us internally and externally.
Now, as it is time to part, may you personally be with us wherever we go. From now on, we must leave with the mission to unite with heaven and raise a new spiritual movement that will develop into a national movement.
This is the time to pledge before you, Father, that we will dedicate Gyeongsangbuk-do with our strength, so I earnestly ask you to take charge and lead us to the place of results where that can happen.
May the grace and love of all things always be with those who care for your will, and I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
